<script type='text/javascript'>
var focusHtml = document.getElementById('focus');
var cookieId = focusHtml.getAttribute('data-focus-cookie');

//	['setting-name', enabled-by-default, has-toggle]
var focusSettings = [
	
 
	['mobile-footer', 1, 1],
	['fluid', 1, 1],
	['larger-font-size', 0, 1],
	['sticky-author-panel', 0, 1],
	['sticky-sidebar', 0, 1],
	['flip-sidebar', 0, 1],
	
	
]; 
for(var i = 0; i < focusSettings.length; i++) {
	var settingName = focusSettings[i][0];
	var isDefault = focusSettings[i][1];
	var allowToggle = focusSettings[i][2];
	if(allowToggle){
		var choice = localStorage.getItem(settingName);
		if( (choice === '1') || (!choice && (isDefault)) ){
			focusHtml.classList.add('enable--' + settingName + '');
		}
	} else if(isDefault){
		focusHtml.classList.add('enable--' + settingName + '');
	}
}

	var loadRandomBackground = function(){
		var randomBackgrounds = [ 1,2,3,4,];
		var randomBackground = randomBackgrounds[Math.floor(Math.random()*randomBackgrounds.length)];
		focusHtml.setAttribute('data-focus-bg', randomBackground);
		focusHtml.setAttribute('data-focus-bg-random', '');
	}


	
		var backgroundChoice = localStorage.getItem('focusBackground-' + cookieId + '') || '1';
		if (backgroundChoice == 'random'){
			loadRandomBackground();
		} else {
			focusHtml.setAttribute('data-focus-bg', '' + backgroundChoice + '');
		}
	

</script>

<script>$(document).ready(function(){
	
	var html = $('#focus');

	if (matchMedia) {
		var focus_pageWidth = window.matchMedia( "(min-width: 980px)" );
		focus_pageWidth.addListener(WidthChange);
		WidthChange(focus_pageWidth);
	}
	function WidthChange(focus_pageWidth) {
		if (focus_pageWidth.matches) {
			$("#elSearchWrapper").prependTo(".focus-search");
		} else {
			$("#elSearchWrapper").prependTo(".focus-mobile-search");
		}
	}

	

	// Customizer
	var customizerTooltip = getComputedStyle(document.documentElement).getPropertyValue('--lang__Customizer').slice(1, -1);
	$('[data-focus-editor] [data-ipsTooltip]').prop('title', customizerTooltip);
	$("[data-focus-editor]").hover(function() {
		html.addClass('focus-picker--loaded');
	});
	// Open and close with data-focus-editor
	$("[data-focus-editor]").on('click', function(event){
		html.toggleClass('focus-editor-open').addClass('focus-picker--loaded');
		event.preventDefault();
	});
	// ..and close by pressing ESC
	$(document).keyup(function(e) {
		if (e.keyCode === 27){
			html.removeClass('focus-editor-open');
		}
	});

	
		// Background Picker
		var selectedPicker = $('.focus-picker__item[data-focus-bg="' + backgroundChoice + '"]');
		selectedPicker.addClass('focus-picker__item--active');

		$(".focus-picker__item").on('click', function(){
			var backgroundClass = $(this).attr("data-focus-bg");
			$('.focus-picker__item').removeClass('focus-picker__item--active');
			$(this).addClass('focus-picker__item--active');
			if (backgroundClass == 'random'){
				html.attr('data-focus-bg-random', '');
			} else {
				html.attr('data-focus-bg', '' + backgroundClass + '');
				html.removeAttr('data-focus-bg-random');
			}
			localStorage.setItem('focusBackground-' + cookieId + '', '' + backgroundClass + '');
		});
	

	// Loop through settings and create the Customizer panels
	for(var i = 0; i < focusSettings.length; i++) {
		if(focusSettings[i][2]){
			var settingName = focusSettings[i][0];
			var settingDefault = focusSettings[i][1];
			var settingChoice = localStorage.getItem(settingName);
			if(settingChoice === '1' || (!(settingChoice) && settingDefault)){
				var status = 1;
			} else {
				var status = 0;
			}
			$("#focusEditorPanels").append("<div class='focus-editor-panel' data-setting='" + settingName + "' data-default='" + settingDefault + "' data-status='" + status + "'><div class='focus-editor-toggle'><i class='focus-toggle'><i></i></i></div><div class='focus-editor-text'></div></div>");
		}
	}

	// Change the class and localstorage when the toggle is clicked
	$('.focus-editor-panel[data-setting]').on('click', function(){
		var settingName = $(this).attr('data-setting');
		var settingStatus = $(this).attr('data-status');
		if(settingStatus === '1'){
			html.removeClass('enable--' + settingName);
			localStorage.setItem(settingName, '0');
			$(this).attr('data-status', '0');
		} else {
			html.addClass('enable--' + settingName);
			localStorage.setItem(settingName, '1');
			$(this).attr('data-status', '1');
		}
	});

	// Dark/light mode button
	var toggleThemeTooltip = getComputedStyle(document.documentElement).getPropertyValue('--lang--light-dark-mode').slice(1, -1);
	$('[data-focus-toggle-theme] [data-ipsTooltip]').prop('title', toggleThemeTooltip);
	$('[data-focus-toggle-theme]').on('click', function(e){
		var focusThemeId = html.attr('data-focus-alt-theme');
		if(focusThemeId){
			e.preventDefault();
			$("#focusAltThemeSubmit").val(focusThemeId);
			$("#focusAltThemeSubmit").click();
		}
	});

	 
		// Make hover navigation work with touch devices
		;(function(e,t,n,r){e.fn.doubleTapToGo=function(r){if(!("ontouchstart"in t)&&!navigator.msMaxTouchPoints&&!navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().match(/windows phone os 7/i))return false;this.each(function(){var t=false;e(this).on("click",function(n){var r=e(this);if(r[0]!=t[0]){n.preventDefault();t=r}});e(n).on("click touchstart MSPointerDown",function(n){var r=true,i=e(n.target).parents();for(var s=0;s<i.length;s++)if(i[s]==t[0])r=false;if(r)t=false})});return this}})(jQuery,window,document); $('.ipsNavBar_primary > ul > li:has(ul)').doubleTapToGo();
	

	

	

	

	

	

	// Toggle class
	$('[data-class]').on( "click", function(event) { event.preventDefault(); var classContent = $(this).attr('data-class'); var classModifiers = classContent.split(' '); var className = classModifiers[0]; var modifyClass = classModifiers[1]; if (classModifiers[2]){ var targetElement = classModifiers[2]; } else { var targetElement = 'html'; } if (modifyClass === 'add'){ $(targetElement).addClass(className); } else if (modifyClass === 'remove'){ $(targetElement).removeClass(className); } else { $(targetElement).toggleClass(className); } });

});

// More dropdown menu
 
function focusNavigation() { var navwidth = 0; var morewidth = $('.ipsNavBar_primary .focus-nav__more').outerWidth(true); $('.ipsNavBar_primary > ul > li:not(.focus-nav__more)').each(function() { navwidth += $(this).outerWidth( true ) + 2; }); var availablespace = $('.ipsNavBar_primary').outerWidth(true) - morewidth; if (availablespace > 0 && navwidth > availablespace) { var lastItem = $('.ipsNavBar_primary > ul > li:not(.focus-nav__more)').last(); lastItem.attr('data-width', lastItem.outerWidth(true)); lastItem.prependTo($('.ipsNavBar_primary .focus-nav__more > ul')); focusNavigation(); } else { var firstMoreElement = $('.ipsNavBar_primary li.focus-nav__more li').first(); if (navwidth + firstMoreElement.data('width') < availablespace) { firstMoreElement.insertBefore($('.ipsNavBar_primary .focus-nav__more')); } } if ($('.focus-nav__more li').length > 0) { $('.focus-nav__more').removeClass('focus-nav__more--hidden'); } else { $('.focus-nav__more').addClass('focus-nav__more--hidden'); } }
$(window).on('load',function(){ $(".ipsNavBar_primary").removeClass("ipsNavBar_primary--loading"); focusNavigation(); });
$(window).on('resize',function(){ focusNavigation(); });
$(document).ready(function(){
	$('[data-setting="fluid"]').on('click', function(){
		setTimeout(function(){
			focusNavigation();
		}, 10);
	});
});

</script>

			<p>
	Hard to believe I’ve come so far in what seems like so little time.
</p>

<p>
	Tonight felt like a huge milestone getting to add detail pieces that really make it feel real.
</p>

<p>
	<u>Jetpack</u>
</p>

<p>
	Decals and Beacon with LED and Stabilizer Added
</p>

<p>
	<u>Jetpack Decals</u>
</p>

<p>
	Purchased from <a href="https://www.etsy.com/listing/634846515/" rel="external nofollow">HerosEnd on Etsy</a> - You will need to message them to ask that 2 extra circles are included.
</p>

<p>
	<img alt="rHCOmnV.jpeg" class="ipsImage" data-ratio="133.33" height="1200" width="1200" src="https://i.imgur.com/rHCOmnV.jpeg" /><br />
	 
</p>

	<img alt="oXV5JHO.jpeg" class="ipsImage" data-ratio="133.33" height="1200" width="1200" src="https://i.imgur.com/oXV5JHO.jpeg" /></p>

<p>
	<img alt="yw9eDoj.jpg" class="ipsImage" data-ratio="133.33" height="1200" width="1200" src="https://i.imgur.com/yw9eDoj.jpg" /><br /><br /><u>Knee Armor</u>
</p>

<p>
	Darts added
</p>

<p>
	<img alt="ftGP8GM.jpeg" class="ipsImage" data-ratio="75.00" height="1200" width="1200" src="https://i.imgur.com/ftGP8GM.jpeg" /><br />

<p>
	<u>Chest and Shoulder Armor</u>

	<div class='cPost_contentWrap'>
		
		<div data-role='commentContent' class='ipsType_normal ipsType_richText ipsPadding_bottom ipsContained' data-controller='core.front.core.lightboxedImages'>
			<p>
	<u>Gauntlets</u>
</p>

<p>
	Fabricated and Painted - <a href="https://www.facebook.com/JandKprops" rel="external nofollow">J&amp;K Props</a>
</p>

<p>
	Gauntlets Model - <a href="https://www.etsy.com/listing/1052295261/" rel="external nofollow">ImperialArmory</a>
</p>

<p>
	Hoses - Amazon - <a href="https://a.co/d/bPFec9J" rel="external nofollow">Sashco-30501 Pre-Caulking Filler Rope Backer Rod, 1/2-Inch x 100-Feet, Grey</a>
</p>

<p>
	Shielding - Amazon - <a href="https://a.co/d/dRcNTML" rel="external nofollow">25ft - 1/2 inch PET Expandable Braided Sleeving – Black – Alex Tech Braided Cable Sleeve</a>
</p>

<p>
	Per CRL: A ⅝ inch (17 mm) rigid hose wrapped tightly in a black braided sleeve.
</p>

<p>
	<span style="background-color:#2e3035;color:#ffffff;font-size:16px;"><img alt="w43GGOG.jpeg" class="ipsImage" src="https://i.imgur.com/w43GGOG.jpeg" /></span>
</p>

<p>
	<span style="background-color:#2e3035;color:#ffffff;font-size:16px;"><a href="https://imgur.com/a/gauntlets-oUfKhiW" rel="external nofollow">More Gauntlet Pics</a></span>
</p>

<p>
	<u>Shoulder Bells and Chest Decals</u>
</p>

<p>
	Added <a href="?ref=ppx_pop_mob_ap_share" rel="">texture paste</a> to decals to blend in and texture shoulder bells. Thanks to <a href="https://thebhg.net/forum/index.php?/profile/15178-iceknyght/" rel="">Iceknyght</a> for the suggestion!
</p>

<p>
	<u><img alt="l965Y3I.jpeg" class="ipsImage" data-ratio="133.33" height="1200" width="1200" src="https://i.imgur.com/l965Y3I.jpeg" /></u>
</p>

<p>
	<img alt="vREMSzL.jpeg" class="ipsImage" data-ratio="75.00" height="1200" width="1200" src="https://i.imgur.com/vREMSzL.jpeg" /></p>

<p>
	<u>All Armor</u>
</p>

<p>
	Used a mix of black acrylic paint, rinse aid, and water to create a black wash to apply to all armor pieces.  Then added metallic paint details.
</p>

<p>
	<u><img alt="yRhBwYi.jpeg" class="ipsImage" data-ratio="133.33" height="1200" width="1200" src="https://i.imgur.com/yRhBwYi.jpeg" /></u>
</p>

			<p>
	<u>Gauntlet Hoses</u>
</p>

<p>
	I used a drill bit to make a hole and then dremmel to widen it out so the magnet will fit to attach the hose connection.
</p>

<p>
	<u><img alt="AytKoS1.jpeg" class="ipsImage" data-ratio="75.00" height="1200" width="1200" src="https://i.imgur.com/AytKoS1.jpeg" /></u><br />
	 
</p>

<p>
	<u><img alt="cz3NhB0.jpeg" class="ipsImage" data-ratio="133.33" height="1200" width="1200" src="https://i.imgur.com/cz3NhB0.jpeg" /></u>
</p>

<p>
	<u><img alt="RTrtRax.jpeg" class="ipsImage" data-ratio="133.33" height="1200" width="1200" src="https://i.imgur.com/RTrtRax.jpeg" /></u><br />
	 
</p>

<p>
	<u><img alt="CNJc5t6.jpeg" class="ipsImage" data-ratio="133.33" height="1200" width="1200" src="https://i.imgur.com/CNJc5t6.jpeg" /></u>
</p>

<p>
	If you have a <span>3D printer you could add a thin wall to the end of the connector which would encase/hide the magnet.  I will do it manually and blend it in.</span>
</p>

	<div class='cPost_contentWrap'>
		
		<div data-role='commentContent' class='ipsType_normal ipsType_richText ipsPadding_bottom ipsContained' data-controller='core.front.core.lightboxedImages'>
			<p>
	Proud to say I am now an approved Bounty Hunter. <a href="https://www.501st.com/members/displaymember.php?userID=10273&amp;costumeID=6" rel="external nofollow">https://www.501st.com/members/displaymember.php?userID=10273&amp;costumeID=6</a>
</p>

<p>
	<br />
	Boba Fett is my favorite character. It is fulfilling a life long dream to be approved and represent him in the 501st Legion and the BHG.
</p>

<p>
	<br />
	I appreciate everyone’s help on this thread who is contributed with guidance on my build. <br />
	 
</p>

<p>
	Thanks to the prop makers for using their talents to make pieces available to the community and for their help in this journey.
</p>

<p>
	Last but not least thanks to <span style="background-color:#121212;color:#878787;font-size:13px;text-align:left;">NoZoupForYou for being the CRL model and sharing their build that we can use as a guide for creating our costumes. </span><br />
	 
</p>

<p>
	I enjoyed documenting my build to help others.  If it helped you react to this post! 
</p>
